Do you have her number?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我正在设法和简<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">取得联系</strong>。你有她的电话号码吗？</p><p </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. realise (also realize America English) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Uk&amp;US/ˈrɪəlaɪz/ verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to understand a situation, sometimes suddenly明白；认识到；意识到</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这个意义上，realise通常不用于进行时态。比如：没有人意识到这有多重要。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">正确：Nobody realizes how important this is.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">错误：Nobody is realizing how important this is.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在英语口语中，人们有时会说我正在意识到他们最近开始意识到某事：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g:Now I’m a parent, I’m realizing what my parents went through.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在我为人父母，我明白我父母所经历的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Word family: (noun) realism realist reality unreality realization</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">         (adjective) real unreal realistic unrealistic（否定）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(verb)realize（realise）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(adverb)real really realistically  unrealistically（否定）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. Don’t be silly.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">意思是 别傻了。（一般应该用于你的朋友有不切实际的想法或是很荒谬的想法）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Beth, would you like me to help you carry it?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Thanks, but I don't want to put you into any trouble.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Don't be silly. It's no trouble at all.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. genealogy </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/ˌdʒiːniˈælədʒi/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(the study of) the history of the past and present members of a family or families家谱（学），宗谱（学）；家系，世系</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">gen-或者gin-主要源自希腊语，部分源自拉丁语，意为birth, gender, family, kind, race</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">genea（基因）+logy（术语后缀，表示…论，… 学，…科，…的言语）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. fascinating </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/ˈfæsəneɪtɪŋ/  adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">extremely interesting极有趣的；吸引人的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g.: That sounds absolutely fascinating. 这听起来绝对令人着迷。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g,:The book offers a fascinating glimpse of the lives of the rich and famous.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这本书使我们得以一窥富豪名流的生活，十分有趣。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g.: I found the whole movie fascinating.我觉得整部电影都很吸引人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. celebrity </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/səˈlebrəti/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">someone who is famous, especially in the entertainment business（尤指娱乐行业的）名人，明星；名流</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Word family: (noun) celebration celebrity</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">         (adjective) celebrated celebratory</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(verb)celebrate</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. a couple of adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">more than one but indefinitely small in number两个, 几个;一对，三两个...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7. descendant </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/dɪˈsendənt/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a person who is related to you and who lives after you, such as your child or grandchild子孙，后代</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">【记忆】descend传下+ant人→传下的人→后代</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8. skeleton in the closet </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">秘密，千万别理解成壁橱中有骷髅。（英国人也会说成skeleton in the cupboard) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">据说当年这个习语产生的时候的确指那些有钱人家谋杀了一个人，把骸骨暗藏在壁橱中，不让外人知道，从此 skeleton in the closet 就成了那家人的秘密。后来这个短语用来形容不可或不愿外扬的家丑，简称作family skeleton。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g.: Many old families have a number of skeletons in their closets which they are loath to discuss。许多古老的家族中有很多秘密，他们不愿谈及这些话题。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9. reckon </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/ˈrekən/ verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to think or believe想；认为，以为</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g.: I reckon it's going to rain.我觉得天要下雨了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">[ + (that) ] How much do you reckon (that) it's going to cost?你认为这会花多少钱？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"Can you fix my car today?" "I reckon not/so (= probably not/probably)."“你能今天把我的汽车修好吗？”“我想不行／大概可以。”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: I'm Catherine…</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">大家好，欢迎收听英语六分钟，我是凯瑟琳。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d I</span></span>'m Neil. Do you realise, Catherine, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span></em> we are relate<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to each other?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我是尼尔。凯瑟琳你知道吗，咱俩是有亲缘关系的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Don't be silly, Neil. I think I'd kn<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ow<sup style="box-sizing: border-box;">(w)</sup> i</span></span>f you w<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ere<sup style="box-sizing: border-box;">(r)</sup> i</span></span>n my family.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">别傻了，尼尔。你要是我们家的人，我肯定会知道的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, we'll talk m<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ore<sup tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> later in the show, bu<span style="text-decoration: genealogy – or the stud<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y<sup style="box-sizing: border-box;">(j)</sup> o</span></span>f family history. An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d I</span></span> thin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k i</span></span>t's pretty fascinating stuff. Do you ever watch the TV programme Who do you think you are, Catherine? You know, where celebrities fin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d ou</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> abou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> their family history?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">稍后，我们再谈这个话题。现在我要说的是，今天我们将讨论宗谱</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">对家族史的研究。我觉得这个话题很吸引人。你看过《你以为你是谁》这个节目吗？这是一些名人寻找自己家族史的节目。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Yeah, I've see<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span> coup<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">le o</span></span>f them. For example, one celebrity – he(who) was very prou<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d of </span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">h</span></span><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">i</span></span>s working class London roots – or origins– discovered <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that</em> he's actually a direct descendant o<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f an E</span></span>nglish king!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我看过几集。例如，一位名人为自己是正宗的伦敦工人阶级而感到骄傲，结果发现自己是货真价实的英国国王的直系后代。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, that's qui<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">te <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</em> </span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">i</span></span>scovery! The thi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng i</span></span>s though, Catherine, wha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> if there isn'<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>nything exciting in your family history– no mysteries, no skeleton<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s i</span></span>n the closet…</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这确实是个大发现！问题是：万一你的家族史里没什么激动人心的事呢？</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没有未解之谜、没有不可告人的秘密</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">……</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Well, I recko<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n i</span></span>f you go back f<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ar<sup style="box-sizing: border-box;">(r)</sup> e</span></span>nough Neil, there's always something exciting or unexpected in anybody's family history. An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> skeleton<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s i</span></span>n the closet by the way, means secrets! Now, I thin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k i</span></span>t's time for today's quiz question.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得如果你追溯到很久很久以前，任何人的家族史都会有一些有意思的或不可思议的事。顺便说一下，</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">skeletons in the closet</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是指秘密。我觉得是时候问今天的问题了。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: Digory in a voice even nastier than he meant it to be; for he saw Polly's hand moving to her pocket to get hold of her yellow ring. I can't excuse what he did next except by saying that he was very sorry for it afterwards (and so were a good many other people). Before Polly's hand reached her pocket, he grabbed her wrist, leaning across with his back against her chest. Then, keeping her other arm out of the way with his other elbow, he leaned forward, picked up the hammer, and struck the golden bell a light, smart tap. Then he let her go and they fell apart staring at each other and breathing hard.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迪格雷看见波莉的手伸向口袋，要去抓那枚黄戒指，便用一种连自己都意想不到的难听声音喊道“住手！”我不能为迪格雷下面的行为开脱，最多只能说，他后来感到抱嗽（许多人都会这样）。在波莉的手摸到口袋以前，他扼住了她的手腕，俯过身去，用背抵住她的胸膛，然后用另一只手的肘部挡开她另一条手臂。他斜着身，拾起小锤，轻快地在钟上敲了一下。然后，他放开她，两人都跌倒在地，喘着气，狠狠地盯着对方。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong><br/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. wouldn't 中的dn可发成鼻腔爆破/dn/，或/<strong style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);font-size: 14px;text-align: left;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">d<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 13px;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">ə</span>n</strong>/。</strong></p><p 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. more than words</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">言语之外；尽在不言中</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I loved you <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">more than words</span></strong></em> can say.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">无法用言语表达</strong>对你的爱。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sometimes there's nothing to say. Sometimes silence expresses <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">more than words</span></em></strong> do.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有时候，不需要说什么，沉默<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">比话语表达得更多</strong>。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I love you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">more than words</span></em></strong> can say.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我爱你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">胜过千言万语</strong> <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;">'Cause that says so much </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">more than words</span></em></strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">因为这<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">比言语更能说明问题</strong>。</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1640.98px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 1640.98px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdSBbUEEib7xPiaK5qicWogz0WXq88pmsObgHCPia0IysPBdDZIzwHfm6nCg6exD8RmpZz3tY6hiaDL0Dw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="939" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《The Office》</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2.  词链儿：all you have to do 你所有需要做的=你唯一要做的</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">All you have to do</span></em></strong> is right-click on the desktop and select New Folder. </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你唯一需要做的</strong>是在桌面上右击鼠标，然后选择“新建文件夹”。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">句式：XX is all you have to do (to...) </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你唯一要做的就是XX，（以达到XX目的）</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>*同do be do句式：all you have to do is (to) do...</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">相同表达：</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">All you have to do is </strong></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">dream</g></strong></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">.</strong></em></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">All you have to do is to dream.</strong></em></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">Dream（noun.）</g></strong></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">is all you have to do.</strong></em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. make it real 使其变得真实</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">make XX adj. 使变得...；使成为...</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The news <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">made him very happy</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这则消息<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">使他非常高兴</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">made her objections clear</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">明确表示反对</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">…<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">make it remarkably easy</span></em></strong> to find Nash Equilibria.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们在寻找纳什均衡时<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">会更容易些</strong>。<span style="text-align: center;font-size: 16px;"></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh,geez.</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(199, 217, 42);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(238, 105, 44);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -43px 0% 43px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 26px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: 6px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这段视频中，出现了两次“炒鱿鱼”这个表达。分别是give XX a heave-ho和fire XX.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>1：Max just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">gave me the heave-ho</strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>2：She said it was the fat girl. And then demanded Max <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fire me</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fire XX这个词链大家都很熟悉啦。我们来重点学习一下give XX a heave-ho这个词链。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个词链不光可以用在想解雇XX的时候，还可以用在想跟XX断绝关系的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If I lost the project, my boss would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">give me a heave-ho</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我要是丢了这个项目，我老板就会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">炒了我</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She just found that her boyfriend cheated on her with the other girl and she<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> gave him a heave-ho </strong>right away.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她刚刚发现她男朋友背着她跟别的女孩偷腥，于是她立马<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">跟他分手了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“炒鱿鱼”还可以怎么说呢？</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: top;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(78, 177, 17);font-size: 18px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get canned </strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: bottom;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">can XX 是“让XX卷铺盖走人”的意思。那么get canned 就是被解雇的意思啦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can't call me manager anymore.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> Just got canned</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别再叫我经理了。我刚<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被炒鱿鱼了</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section You're nice to everybody. It had to have been one of the other girl.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">B</strong>: No. She said it was the fat girl. And then demanded Max<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> fire me</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">A</strong>: Who the hell is this <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">on board</strong>?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">B</strong>: She wouldn't give Max her name.But he still believed her, so to hell with him and this crummy job.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">A</strong>: Is there some lady out there who <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">hates your guts</strong>?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh,geez.</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 12.5%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(-15px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-15px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-15px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-15px, 0px, 0px);margin: 12px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 12px;height: 12px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: top;width: 12.5%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 42);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 12.5%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 80px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(254, 239, 158);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 12.5%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 80px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 12.5%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 80px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(238, 105, 44);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 217, 73);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(199, 217, 42);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 55px;height: 55px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 72px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(238, 105, 44);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -43px 0% 43px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(2px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 26px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: 6px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链精解</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这段视频中，出现了两次“炒鱿鱼”这个表达。分别是give XX a heave-ho和fire XX.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>1：Max just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">gave me the heave-ho</strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>2：She said it was the fat girl. And then demanded Max <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fire me</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fire XX这个词链大家都很熟悉啦。我们来重点学习一下give XX a heave-ho这个词链。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个词链不光可以用在想解雇XX的时候，还可以用在想跟XX断绝关系的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If I lost the project, my boss would <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">give me a heave-ho</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我要是丢了这个项目，我老板就会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">炒了我</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She just found that her boyfriend cheated on her with the other girl and she<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> gave him a heave-ho </strong>right away.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她刚刚发现她男朋友背着她跟别的女孩偷腥，于是她立马<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">跟他分手了</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“炒鱿鱼”还可以怎么说呢？</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: top;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(78, 177, 17);font-size: 18px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get canned </strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: bottom;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">can XX 是“让XX卷铺盖走人”的意思。那么get canned 就是被解雇的意思啦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can't call me manager anymore.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> Just got canned</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别再叫我经理了。我刚<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被炒鱿鱼了</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: top;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(142, 201, 101);font-size: 18px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get laid off </strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: bottom;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He had<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> been laid off </strong>only hours earlier.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">几个小时前，他才刚<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被解雇</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: top;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(142, 201, 101);font-size: 18px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be made redundant</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: bottom;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Without any notice, we were all suddenly <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">made redundant</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们突然都<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被解雇了</strong>，没有任何通知。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: top;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(142, 201, 101);font-size: 18px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get the sack</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40px;vertical-align: bottom;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 181, 97);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(119, 174, 76);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">got the sack </strong>for swearing. 他因说脏话而<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">被开除。</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: perspective(0px);-webkit-transform: perspective(0px);-moz-transform: perspective(0px);-o-transform: perspective(0px);transform-style: flat;box-sizing: border-box;"><section </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">involve </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/in'vɔlv/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 包含；牵涉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It involves dozens of countries from around the world.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">全球数十个国家参与其中。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Interactional fairness involves treating people with dignity and respect.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">互动公平包括给他人尊严、尊重他人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">document</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'dɒkjʊm(ə)nt/ /ˈdɑkjəmənt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 文件，公文；文档；证件</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 用文件证明</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That document was the Declaration of Independent.那份文件是《独立宣言》。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Certificates</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/sə'tɪfɪkət/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> n. 证明书, 执照</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you have any certificates on computer?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">您有计算机等级证书吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I have NCRE (National Computer Rank Examination) certificate, Rank II.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我有全国计算机等级考试的二级证书。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">de·cipher </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ dɪˈsaɪfə(r) /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 破译(密码), 辨认(潦草字迹)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That was the train of events as far as I can decipher them.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是我所能推想出来的一些情况。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't decipher the words to many of the popular songs I love, either.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有很多我喜欢的流行歌词我也搞不明白。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be difficult to 难以；做……很困难</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It may be difficult to do at first. Don't let this discourage you.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">开始时做起来也许比较困难。不要因为这个令你泄气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The scientists admit their goal will be difficult to achieve.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">科学家们承认他们的目标很难实现。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">con·nect </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ kəˈnekt /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> vt. 连接；联合；关连</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 连接，连结；联合</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Thank you for waiting. I'll connect you.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">让你久等了，我帮你接通。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Vietnamese connect their smartphones to wireless Internet.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们用智能手机连接无线网络上网。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">digitize</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'didʒitaiz/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 数码化</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The first challenge is to recognise and digitise speech.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第一个难题是识别声音并数字化。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">avail·able / əˈveɪləbl / ADJECTIVE</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 可用的或可得到的,可会见的, 可与之交谈的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The carpet is available in different widths.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这款地毯有各种宽度可供选择。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">rustling</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 沙沙作响的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A rustling sound came from outside the window.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一阵沙沙声从窗外传来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sheep rustling looms larger as a result.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Researching family history ofte<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n i</span></span>nvolves reading ol<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>documents su<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ch a</span></span>s birth, marriage and death certificates, an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> these can be difficult to decipher – or understand. So what's the name for the study of ancient handwriting? Is it…a) Scriptography? b) Palaeography? Or c) Scribology?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">调查家族史时，通常会参照古老文献，如出生证明、结婚证或死亡证明，这些都是很难理解的文献。那么，研究古代手稿的学科叫什么？</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) Scriptography</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">？</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">b) Palaeography </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">（古文书学）？还是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">c) Scribology</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> mus<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> be a) Scriptography.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">一定是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) Scriptography</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> we'll see if you're righ<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span>r no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> late<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r o</span></span>n in the show. Now, why do you think most people loo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k i</span></span>nto their genealogy, Neil? Is i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> jus<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> curiosity?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">稍后，我们再看你的回答是否正确。尼尔，为什么大多数人都喜欢调查自己的宗谱呢？只是出于好奇吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, Catherine, w<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e a</span></span>ll lo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ve a</span></span> goo<span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span> mystery story – especially i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f i</span></span>t's connecte<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> wi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">th o</span></span>u<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r o</span></span>wn family. An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> these days, i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t's ea</span></span>sy to do research online because many old paper documents have been digitised an<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>re available online.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们都喜欢富有神秘感的故事</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">尤其是和自己的家人有关的。近来，人们能轻松地在网上搜寻信息，因为网上有很多古老纸质文献的电子版。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: BBC presenter Mike Williams investigated hi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>wn family history. An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d </span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">h</span></span></span>ere, he's talki<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng a</span></span>bou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> his great-grandfather's story. An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>f you listen carefully you can hear him rustling the real paper documents!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">BBC</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">主持人麦克</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">威廉姆斯调查了他自己的家族史。接下来他会讲述他曾外祖父的故事。如果你认真听，你可以听到翻纸质文献时的沙沙声。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">The Williamses are my father's side and on my mother's the Heino's – <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">it's a</span></span> name tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> we think comes from Finland.</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">威廉姆斯是我父亲这边的姓，我母亲这边姓海诺，我们觉得这个名字来自芬兰。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As soon as the bell was struck it gave out a note, a sweet note such as you might have expected, and not very loud. But instead of dying away again, it went on; and as it went on it grew louder. Before a minute had passed it was twice as loud as it had been to begin with. It was soon so loud that if the children had tried to speak (but they weren't thinking of speaking now - they were just standing with their mouths open) they would not have heard one another. Very soon it was so loud that they could not have heard one another even by shouting.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">钟刚刚敲晌的时候，就发出一种音调，不太响亮，但你可以想像，声音很甜美。这种音调非但没有减弱，反而继续鸣响，而且越来越响，在不到一分钟的时间里，音调就比刚开始时响亮一倍。声音迅速增长到如果孩子们想说话（但他们当时并未想到说话一一他们只是张口结舌地站着）,互相之间也无法听见的程度。顷刻间，声音响得即使他们大声喊叫也听不见了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 什么风把你吹来？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我来看我姨妈。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 她住在这附近？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是的，她就住在下个街区。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Well, what brings you here?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I came to see my aunt.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Does she live nearby?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. She lives on the next block.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If the cost of the trip is no more than 1000 yuan, you can _____________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果这次旅行的花费不超过一千元，就算我一个。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">count me in</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">8.11 早读原文</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom:
