style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">When you're used to <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">privilege</g>, equality feels like oppression.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. used /juːst/ <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. oppression /əˈpreʃən/ -ssion 对应的发音</strong></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(337.547px, 985.906px);-webkit-transform: translate(337.547px, 985.906px);-moz-transform: translate(337.547px, 985.906px);-o-transform: translate(337.547px, 985.906px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿: be/get used to (doing) XX 习惯于(做)某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I do the dishes every day, so I'<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">m used to</span></em></strong> it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我每天洗盘子，所以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">习惯</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">m</span></em></strong> not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">used to</span></em></strong> eating so much at lunchtime.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">习惯</strong>午饭吃那么多。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong> If your company <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">is used to</span></em></strong> doing things in a particular way...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果你的公司<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">习惯于</strong>以特定的方式做事...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I'<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">m</span></em></strong> not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">used to </span></em></strong>being interrupted by applause.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">习惯</strong>被掌声打断。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展：used /juːzd/ adj. 用过的；旧的；二手的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">used cars 二手汽车</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a used tissue 用过的纸巾</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">*注意区分<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be/get used to (doing) XX 变得习惯于(做)某事和used to do XX 过去常常做某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tom <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong><em>wasn’t</em></strong></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">used to</span></em></strong> noise. It took him some time to <em><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>get used to</strong></span> </em>it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汤姆之前并不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">习惯于</strong>噪音，一段时间后他才开始习惯。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> And I'<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">m used to</span></em></strong> people calling me names.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我已经<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">习惯</strong>别人的辱骂了。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6231481" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdSBbUEEib7xPiaK5qicWogz0Wq0OFtkm4PWjCP8X3Z4xAlHSGgKn7mYd5c2U59OdrDM0fAnIU728Wzw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《家有正太》</span></p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">used to</span></em></strong> play with my friends after school.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">过去放学后我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">常常</strong>和朋友们一起玩。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">used to</span></em></strong> keep one as a pet.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">以前</strong>养过一只当宠物。 </p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 2058.23px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 2058.23px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 2058.23px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 2058.23px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6138889" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdSBbUEEib7xPiaK5qicWogz0WdPwH8U62f3DPTUibFg83GOQ5IQIrb1y2qpoRFt4kIeTbREY4CJjLkXg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《美国恐怖故事》</span></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. privilege noun.</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→特权，特殊待遇</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">privilege</span></em></strong> of a good education</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">可以享受良好教育的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">特权</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ 荣幸；幸运</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I hope to have the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">privilege</span></em></strong> of working with them again.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但愿有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">幸</strong>与他们再度合作。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was a great <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">privilege</span></em></strong> to hear her sing.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">听她唱歌真是三生有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">幸</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. equal-equality-inequality</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">equal adj. 平等的，相等的</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Our constitution states that all men are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">equal</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们的宪法规定人人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">平等</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">equality noun. 平等；均等；相等</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't you believe <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">in </g><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">equality</g></span></em></strong> between men and women?</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">难道你不相信男女<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">平等</strong>吗？</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">inequality noun. 不公平</strong></span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There are <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">inequalities</span></em></strong> in wealth distribution.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">财富分配<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不平等</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">inequalities</span></em></strong> between men and women</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">男女间的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不平等</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. oppress verb. 压迫；欺压；压制</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">oppression noun.  压迫，压制 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">victims of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">oppression</span></em></strong> 受<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">压迫</strong>者</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Where there is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">oppression</span></em></strong> there is resistance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">哪里有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">压迫</strong>哪里就有反抗。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Excuse me. What about the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">oppression</span></em></strong> of my people?</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抱歉，那我的人遭受<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">压迫</strong>该怎么办？</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6148148" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdSBbUEEib7xPiaK5qicWogz0WFibCuWGQuJala7yryvoyomOoeUNyv8Kj6ibrfOqpsNlYWobaGoH7YOWg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《查理的战争》</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I see them as the uniform of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">oppression</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在我眼里它们等同于<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">压迫</strong>。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 3664.86px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 3664.86px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. census </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈsensəs/ n.人口普查；人口调查；（官方的）统计</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">scientific census-takers 科学普查者；科学调查员</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. the head of the household 一家之主</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Household Registration户口名簿 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. surname </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈsɜːneɪm $ ˈsɜːr-/ n.姓</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：the name that you share with your parents.SYN last name, family name</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">反义：→ forename</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. originally  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/əˈrɪdʒɪnəli, -dʒənəli/ adv.原来；起初</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">origin /ˈɒrɪdʒɪn $ ˈɔː-, ˈɑː-/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">original /əˈrɪdʒɪnəl, -dʒənəl/</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We had originally gone to the area looking for it. 我们原本是去寻找它的。——《大西洋帝国》</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. pass down 传递</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pass on 传递；传授</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you know what legacy means? It’s what you pass down to your children, and your children’s children. 知道何为家业吗？就是你留给子子孙孙，世代相传的东西。——《权力的游戏》</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. lore </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/lɔː $ lɔːr/ n.传说</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：knowledge or information about a subject, for example nature or magic, that is not written down but is passed from person to person</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the old lore 古老的传说</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">family lore 家族传说</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7. permission  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/pəˈmɪʃən $ pər-/ n.许可；批准；准许；许可证</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">permission from </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You'll have to get permission from your parents if you want to come.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">permission of</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Photographs should only be taken with the permission of the subject.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8. immigration </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˌɪmɪˈɡreɪʃən/ n.移居；外来移民；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Immigration reached its peak in the 1950s.移民在20世纪50年代达到顶峰。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9. fascinated  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈfæsɪneɪtɪd/ adj.入迷的；极感兴趣的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Be fascinated by</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was fascinated by her voice.我被她的声音迷住了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10. Investigate </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ɪnˈvestɪɡeɪt/ v.调查；研究；调查（某人）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The state police are investigating the incident.州警察正在调查这起事件。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">11. saliva  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/səˈlaɪvə/n.唾液;口水</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">One study suggests it may be spread in saliva.一项研究表明，它可能通过唾液传播。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span border-box;"> </span></span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Wednesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">If I loo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">k a</span></span>t this document here – <span style="color: rgb(247, 150, 70);box-sizing: border-box;">it's a</span> copy of the censu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>f England and Wales 1911 - you can see my grandfather, the son, and his father – the hea<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">d of the</span></span> household – Michael Heino, or Michel Heino, who, the family law ha<span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">s i</span>t, jum<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">ped</span></span> shi<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">p</span></span> and end<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">ed up in</span></span> Liverpool.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">该文献是英格兰和威尔士</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">1911</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">年人口普查的复印版。文献里记载了我的外祖父（也就是我曾外祖父的儿子）和他的父亲迈克尔</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">海诺</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">一家之主，他跳下了船，然后生活在了利物浦。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: What's a census, Catherine?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">census</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是什么意思呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: It's an official coun<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span>f people i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span> population. So Mike Williams' grea<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> grandfather appeare<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">d o</span></span>n the 1911 census for Englan<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>nd Wales but becau<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">se o</span></span>f his surname the family think he might originally have come from Finland.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这是官方统计出的人口数。所以麦克</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">威廉姆斯的曾外祖父出现在了英格兰和威尔士</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">1911</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">年的人口普查记录中，但因为他的姓，家人一直以为他来自芬兰。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: The exciting event in Mike Williams' history – pass<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span> down through family lore – which means knowledge pass<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">ed o</span></span>n from one generation to the next– <span style="color: rgb(247, 150, 70);box-sizing: border-box;">is that his</span> great-grandfather jum<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">ped</span></span> ship.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在麦克</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">威廉姆斯的族历史中，他曾外祖父跳船的趣事成了家族传说被流传下来，也就是说这段故事被代代相传。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Which means he lef<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the shi<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">p</span></span> he was working on withou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> permission to do so.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">也就是说他未经允许就离开了他工作的船只。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: And he starte<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span> new life in England. I suppose qui<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">te a</span></span> few people have immigration stories in their family histories – sometimes without knowing it.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">然后在英格兰开启了新生活。我觉得很多人的家族史上都有移民史，只是有时他们并不知道。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Actually that's something <span style="color: rgb(247, 150, 70);box-sizing: border-box;">that </span>many peop<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">le are</span></span> fascinated by – <span style="color: rgb(247, 150, 70);box-sizing: border-box;">and has</span> also become easier to investigate these days now companies offer to test the DNA in your saliva for as little a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 80, 77);box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> hundred dollars.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">实际上，这也是人们痴迷于调查家族史的原因。如今，调查家族史也变得很容易了，一些公司可以检测你唾液中的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">DNA</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，费用仅一百美元。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And still it grew: all on one note, a continuous sweet sound, though the sweetness had something horrible about it, till all the air in that great room was throbbing with it and they could feel the stone floor trembling under their feet. Then at last it began to be mixed with another sound, a vague, disastrous noise which sounded first like the roar of a distant train, and then like the crash of a falling tree. They heard something like great weights falling.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">连绵不断的甜美的声音一直在不停地增大，虽然甜美之中透出一丝恐怖的气氛。渐渐地，整个房间的空气也随着那种声音颇动起来，直到两人觉得脚下的石头地板在颤抖。最后，另一种模糊的、灾难性的声音掺合了进来，起初像远方火车的吼叫，接着，又像树木倒下的声音。他们听见似乎有什么重东西在往下倒。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你终于来了！知道吗，你晚了半小时。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 非常抱歉让你等这么久。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 发生什么事了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我的表停了，而我不知道。我真有必要买块好点儿的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Here you are at last! You're half an hour late, you know.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm awfully sorry to have kept you waiting for so long.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What happened?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: My watch stopped and I didn't know. I certainly need to buy a better one.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't help laughing every time I think of that.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每次一想起那件事，我就会_______笑起来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">忍不住</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. wake </strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">up</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">重音在up上；动词+介词的搭配，重音一般均落在后词上；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. </strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">there</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">'ll 为单音节缩约词，此处there弱读为/<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 13px;text-align: start;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">ðə(r)</span>/。</strong></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 998.906px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 998.906px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 998.906px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 998.906px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：wake up 醒来；唤醒</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What time do you usually <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">wake up </span></em></strong>in the morning?</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">通常你早晨几点钟<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">醒</strong>？</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">亦可用作：wake XX up  使活跃；使清醒</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Try not to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">wake</span></em></strong> the baby <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">up</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">尽量别把孩子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">弄醒</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A cold shower will soon <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">wake</span></em></strong> you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">up</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你冲个凉水澡，很快就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">清醒</strong>了。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：less of... （与不可数名词连用）较少的，更少的</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I aim to spend <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">less of</span></em></strong> my time <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">travelling</g>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我打算<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">少</strong>花点时间在旅行上。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Less of</span></em></strong> that noise, please!</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">小点</strong>声！</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">less of</span></em></strong> you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">更少的</strong>你</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿：not even 连...都不</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She did <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">not even</span></em></strong> bother to phone us.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她甚至<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">连</strong>电话<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">都没</strong>打给我们。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">didn’t even</span></em></strong> offer me a cup of tea.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">连</strong>一杯茶<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">都不</strong>给我。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">People were <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">not even</span></em></strong> thinking in scientific ways.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">甚至不</strong>用科学的方式思考。<span style="text-align: center;font-size: 16px;"></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: border-box;">4. 词链儿：care about 在乎，在意；关心</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">care about</span></em></strong> him and hate to see him hurt like this.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">喜欢</strong>他，不看到他这样受伤。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He doesn't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">care about</span></em></strong> his clothes.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">讲究</strong>衣着。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>We <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">care about</span></em></strong> making government work better.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关心</strong>的是让政府工作得更好。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>People <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">care about</span></em></strong> my feelings and they respect me.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在意</strong>我的感受，他们尊重我。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What they <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">care about</span></em></strong> is efficiency and they <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>care about </strong></em></span><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">safety</g>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们真正<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在意</strong>的是效率和安全。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: And then they <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">come up </span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">with </em>results saying you're relat<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> to</em> Alexander <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the </em>Great<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> or</em> Brad Pitt…Remember I said <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that </em>we were related? Well, let's now listen <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to </em>Else Churchill, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">from the </em>Society<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> of</em> Genealogists <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">here in</span></span> London, who explains <span style="text-decoration: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">然后他们会说你和亚历山大大帝有关系，或和布拉德</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">皮特有关系。还记得我之前说的吗，咱俩也有亲缘关系。现在我们来听听伦敦系谱学家协会的埃尔斯</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">丘吉尔怎么解释我的意思。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">There's <span style="color: rgb(18, 18, 18);box-sizing: border-box;">wha</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> <span style="color: rgb(18, 18, 18);box-sizing: border-box;">you </span>might call <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the </em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">gateway </strong>ancestor– <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">and the </em><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">idea <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of</em></span></span> history <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">and </em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">genealogy </strong>is that's normally somebody <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that is </em>so well documented <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that their </em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">descendants </strong><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">are </em>well known – <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">in England </span></span>it's something like Edward III. And <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">we're all </span></span>probably <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">descended </strong>from Edward III. Is it nice <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to </em>have <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">royal ancestors</span></span>? Well, millions<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> of </em>people <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">are </em>descended from Edward III, and<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;"> so in </span></span>that sense,</strong> that's where <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the </em>connection might be. <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">So the</em> chances <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">are an</span></span></em><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">awfu</strong></span></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">l </strong>lot of people are distantly connect<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to </em>each other.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你可能会把这称为祖先，而历史和宗谱通常是指被详细记载以至后代都很出名的某些人</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在英国，爱德华三世就是这样的祖先。我们也许都是爱德华三世的后代。有这样一个王室祖先是不是感觉不错？数百万人都是爱德华三世的后代。所以在这种情况下，人和人之间会存在一些联系。所以，可能很多人彼此之间都有遥远的联系。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></strong></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Else Churchill says it's likely <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">tha<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span></em>millions <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of </em>us are distantly related <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to a g</em>ateway ancestor like King Edward III <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of </em>England. And that means <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that </em>all those people related <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to </em>Edward III <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">are </span></span></em><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">also </span></span>distantly related <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> each other. So it seems <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that </em>paying a company a hundred dollars to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">reveal</strong> that you're related to Edward III is a <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">waste of </span></span>money.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">埃尔斯</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">丘吉尔说，数百万人可能与英国国王爱德华三世这样的祖先有着遥远的关系。也就是说，凡是和爱德华三世有关的人，彼此之间都有遥远的联系。由此看来，你给一个公司一百美元，然后你被告知你和爱德华三世有关，这很浪费钱啊。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Yes, in the sense that it's you and millions <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of </em>other people. And in fact, <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">we're all </span></span>related to each other somehow, via Edward III <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">or </em>someone else.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没错，在这种情况下，你和数百万人都有联系。实际上，我们会因为爱德华三世或其他人而彼此有联系。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Finally, with a sudden, rush and thunder, and a shake that nearly flung them off their feet, about a quarter of the roof at one end of the room fell in, great blocks of masonry fell all round them, and the walls rocked. The noise of the bell stopped. The clouds of dust cleared away. Everything became quiet again. It was never found out whether the fall of the roof was due to Magic or whether that unbearably loud sound from the bell just happened to strike the note which was more than those crumbling walls could stand. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">突然，一阵晃动几乎将他们抛了出去。随着轰隆隆的冲击声，房间一头大约四分之的屋顶塌了下来，大块大块的砖石落在他们周围，墙壁开始摇晃。钟声停止后，灰尘消散，一切又归于宁静。不知道是魔法使屋顶塌了下来，还是响亮的钟声恰好使墙壁无法忍受而崩塌。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 恐怕我不能按时完成论文了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 怎么了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我在实验中不断地遇到困难，几乎做不下去了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 哪儿有困难，哪儿就有解决问题的办法。坚持住！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'm afraid I can't complete my paper on time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What happened?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I keep on meeting with difficulties in the experiment. I can hardly go on.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Where there are difficulties, there are ways to get over them. Hold on!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You can't count on the weather being fine.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. be called XX 名叫，叫作；把…唤作</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Our son <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">is called</span></strong></em> Matthew.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们的儿子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">叫</strong>马修。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. “七夕节”的英文说法：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Double Seventh Festival; </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Chinese Valentine's Day; </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Qixi Festival ; </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Qiqiao Festival</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;">往期相关推文回顾：</span></p><p popular 变得受喜爱的；受欢迎的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Skiing has <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">popular</span></em></strong> recently.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">滑雪运动最近<strong style="box-sizing: increasingly <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">popular</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">辛辣食物越来越<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">受欢迎</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: I might get in with the popular kids.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">变得受欢迎</strong>，和校园名人打成一片。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdxXQhInJYBhTpS2VUZg3bPY1KGm3GGLI4iaJff23Lp1p9ibpwia4X0BP2paRE3GSHCtt8F3iacukKXeg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《龙虎少年队》</span></p><p style="text-align: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. the traditional elder generation 思想传统的老一辈</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the younger generation 年轻的一代</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">the older/elder generation 老一辈</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">*词汇辨析：elder &amp; older</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">elder与eldest主要指家中兄弟姐妹的排行，也可以用older与oldest。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">也就是说，在表示年龄大小方面，elder和older可替换。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">my <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">elder</span></em></strong> / <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">older</span></em></strong> brother 我的哥哥</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">her <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">eldest </span></em></strong>/ <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">oldest</span></em></strong> boy 她的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大</strong>儿子</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> …your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">elder</span></em></strong> sister's wedding. She looked very glamorous.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你姐姐结婚时的照片，她很漂亮。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6231481" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdxXQhInJYBhTpS2VUZg3bPRHsPHTFLVYskzaFohd7vNIItAkV5e5D5a0CXqp4vA2Z0Bic80zPyfSg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">*注意：elder不能后面加上than做比较，要用older。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">older</span></em></strong> than I am. 他年纪比我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但elder还可用来表示地位高、阅历深。older没有此层含义。而且elder可用作名词，表示”先辈“或”年长的人“，而older无此用法。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is an <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">elder</span></em></strong> statesman.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他是一位政治<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">元老</strong>/<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">资深</strong>政客。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the tribal <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">elders</span></em></strong>  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">部落<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">长老</strong>们</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">Special love is for special YOU!</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">至尊宝和紫霞仙子的故事我们都听过，</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">最经典的台词莫过于——</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em><strong>我的意中人是一个盖世英雄。 <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>上天既然安排他拔出我的紫青宝剑， <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>他一定是个不平凡的人， <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>错不了！ <br anybody.</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">我爱你的原因很多，但最重要的原因是你就是你，不是其他任何人。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="white-space: style="box-sizing: border-box;">what you</strong> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">make of it</strong>. <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You are everything to me.</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我所知道的是，我的未来每天<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">有你参与</strong>就足够了,因为你就是我的全部。</span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin-top:
