4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">descend </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 遗传；下去; 下降；下来；   （反义词：ascend 上升）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">descend: 通常指沿斜线或斜坡下降。 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">drop: 指物体从一定高度落下。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fall: 与drop同义，指突然或猛烈地降落，但fall也可指任何下落，同高度或形式无关。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sink: 指在空气或水中垂直下降、下沉。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-ogy 学（构成名词）  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">genealogy 家谱学    biology 生物学     psychology心理学   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">decipher vt. 破译(密码), 辨认(潦草字迹)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can anyone decipher his handwriting?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">date  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v：记载日期于、鉴定…的年代         常用搭配date from 追溯到；始于；起源于</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">date  n：日期、约会</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">up to date adj. 最新的；最近的；现代的       out of date 过时的；过期的；废弃的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">blind date n. 相亲</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">date: 主要指朋友之间的随便约见或男女之间的约会。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">engagement: 泛指任何商定的地点和时间见面，专指针对某一目的约会。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">appointment: 通常指严格根据时间表上预约的时间进行的约见或约会，其目的主要是讨论公事或业务问题。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">skeleton in the cupboard/closet，本意是“柜子里的骷髅”，引申义指“不宜外扬的家丑”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lore  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 知识；学问；全部传说</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But largely, it's a book of childhood memories and family lore</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center center;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: 0.5em;border-top-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Friday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>nother popular finding for British people is to say that you're descende<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> from the Vikings, and again this is true for lots of people</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">so it isn<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">'t</span></span> particularly meaningful.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在英国，另一种流行的说法是：你是维京人的后代。同样，很多人都确实是维京人的后代，所以这也就没什么特别的意义了</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: If you're descende<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> from a person o<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r a</span></span> group it means they are among your ancestors.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">如果你是某个人或某个族群的后代，这就意味着他们是你的祖先之一。</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Now, remember I asked: what's the name <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">for</em> the study of ancient handwriting? Is it… a) Scriptography?    b) Palaeography?   Or    c) Scribology?</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">还记得我之前问的问题吗，研究古代手稿的学科叫什么？</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) Scriptography</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">？</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> b) Palaeography</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">？还是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> c) Scribology?</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I said a) Scriptography. <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span></em> I'm pretty confident that's the right answer.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我选的是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Scriptography</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。我很自信，这就是正确答案。</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Well, Neil, you're pretty confiden<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> but unfortunately i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> was wrong! The correct answer is b) Palaeography. Palaeography is the study of ancient and historical handwriting, including the practice of deciphering, reading, and dating historical manuscripts.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你确实很自信，不过很遗憾，这不是正确答案。正确答案是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">b) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">古文书学。古文书学是研究古代手稿的学科，其中包括破译、阅读和注明历史手稿的日期。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Oh well, here are the words we learned:</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好了，我们来看看今天学到的单词：</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">genealogy</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">宗谱，系谱学</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">roots</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">根源</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">skeletons in the closet</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">秘密</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">decipher</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">破译</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">census</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">人口普查</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">family lore</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">家庭传说</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">descende<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> from</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">起源于</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: And that's the end of today's 6 Minute English. Don't forget to join us again soon!</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">今天的六分钟英语就到这里。欢迎继续收听我们下期节目。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">再见！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">6 Minute English from the BBC.</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">BBC</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">英语六分钟。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">THE children were facing one another across the pillar where the bell hung, still trembling, though it no longer gave out any note. Suddenly they heard a soft noise from the end of the room which was still undamaged. They turned quick as lightning to see what it was. One of the robed figures, the furthest-off one of all, the woman whom Digory thought so beautiful, was rising from its chair. When she stood up they realized that she was even taller than they had thought. And you could see at once, not only from her crown and robes, but from the flash of her eyes and the curve of her lips, that she was a great queen. She looked round the room and saw the damage and saw the children, but you could not guess from her face what she thought of either or whether she was surprised. She came forward with long, swift strides.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然钟声停止了，但钟仍然颤抖着；两个孩子隔普挂钟的柱子面面相觑。忽然，从还没有毁坏的屋子一角传来一阵轻柔的声音。他们立即转身看去。所有穿长袍的塑像中最远的那个，即迪格雷认为非常美丽的女人，正从椅子上站起来。当她站起来后，他们意识到，她比他们原来想像的还要高。而且，从她的王冠、长袍、眼神和嘴唇的线条上，你马上便能看出，她是一位了不起的女王。她环视屋子当中毁坏的场面，也看见了孩子们，但你无法从她脸上的表情判断她是否感到惊讶。她大步流星地走了过来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 哈利，立刻到这儿来！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 有什么事吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 别给我来这样的腔调。我看见你打你弟弟了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不是的！是他先打我的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我不管。你知道你不该打他的。去，到你房间床上静坐十分钟。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Harry, come here immediately!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Don't take that tone with me! I saw you hit your brother.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No! He hit me first.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I don't care. You know better than to hit him. Go sit on your bed for 10 minutes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I didn't catch what you said, please repeat it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我_________你说什么，请重复。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没听清楚</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="text-align: We don't get a lot of things toreallycare about."> about.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">there’ll 包含几个音节？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 1  B 2</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653553589&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=e74de616404df26188e6cb90b435910c&amp;chksm=f7ebc378c09c4a6e9978a6b4b74e6691d19d3ebc6edbbb260f4e85473fca18b67cfdaaab5cb7&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="5. The Double Seventh Festival is called Chinese Valentine's Day and becomes popular among both the traditional elder generation and the young people in life. ">5. The Double Seventh Festival is called Chinese Valentine's Day and becomes popular among both the traditional elder generation and the young people in life. </a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">both the 之间的语音现象为（）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A 省前留后  B 前进同化  C 后进同化</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(341px, 1820.5px);-webkit-transform: translate(341px, 1820.5px);-moz-transform: translate(341px, 1820.5px);-o-transform: translate(341px, 1820.5px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本周知识点回想</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.  预言似乎成真了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.  他并不真正了解年轻人现在对什么感兴趣。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.  我无法用言语表达对你的爱。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.  你唯一需要做的是在桌面上右击鼠标。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.  我每天洗盘子，所以习惯了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.  听她唱歌真是三生有幸。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.  我打算少花点时间在旅行上。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.  他不讲究衣着。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.  滑雪运动最近盛行起来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.  他是一位政治元老。</p></section></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(357px, 2154.5px);-webkit-transform: translate(357px, 2154.5px);-moz-transform: translate(357px, 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section 100%;"></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;font-size: 18px;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When We Two Parted</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">背景音乐：</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">Josh Leake - A Quiet Departure</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;margin-left: 0px;"><img data-ratio="1.002008" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKebunUMV0J8xQ7jDklqnibuxIIC99icqTvWG0qlmRje6Rl7pLgKia94k2LHkQzADdx0FFVkm1NvXiczpA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="498" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section></section><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">作者：拜伦<br/></p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">翻译：佚名</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">朗读：Gwen</p><section><br/></section><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>When we two parted<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>In silence and tears,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Half broken-hearted<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>To sever for years,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Pale grew thy cheek and cold,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Colder thy kiss;<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Truly that hour foretold<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Sorrow to this.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你我离别的时刻<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>沉默与泪水肆虐<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>心近乎绝望的碎裂<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>碎片辗过一大段的岁月<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你的脸颊白如纸而冷若冰<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>给我的寒洌之吻<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>此时此刻已经写下<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>如今伤痛的预言<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>2<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>The dew of the morning<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Sunk chill on my brow —<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>It felt like the warning<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Of what I feel now.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Thy vows are all broken,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>And light is thy fame:<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>I hear thy name spoken,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>And share in its shame.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>早晨的寒露<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>为眉弯添上透骨的寒凉<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>想来是个先兆<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>预告我现今的心境<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>誓言不复存在<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你因冶荡艳名远播<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>惊闻你艳名狼藉<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我的心因羞愧而流血</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>3<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>They name thee before me,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>A knell to mine ear;<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>A shudder comes o'er me —<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Why wert thou so dear?<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>They know not I knew thee,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Who knew thee too well: —<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Long, long shall I rue thee,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Too deeply to tell.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>人们纷纷议论着你的浪荡<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>恶意的评语几乎刺穿双耳<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我颤抖了---<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你我曾是那么的亲密！<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>没人知道你和我相识----<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>而我曾是那么的了解你<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>现在心痛追悔是否太迟<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>又有谁说得清呢！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>4<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>In secret we met —<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>In silence I grieve,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>That thy heart could forget,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>Thy spirit deceive.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>If I should meet thee<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>After long years,<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>How should I greet thee? —<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>With silence and tears.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>终于你我私下再度重逢--<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我卸不去悲戚的秘密桎梏<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你的心抛弃了旧情<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>你的灵魂选择了欺谩<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>要是你我有缘<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>在多年以后再次相见<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>何以致侯？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>以无言的泪水相对而已。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.2162162" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKebunUMV0J8xQ7jDklqnibuxSntYo4kPGIvuQfYAsxWic8AshP1BKLSjwcjxCbpGMXgwnKKkibkeNb7g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="370" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">乔治·戈登·拜伦（George Gordon Byron，1788年1月22日—1824年4月19日），是英国19世纪初期伟大的浪漫主义诗人，代表作品有《恰尔德·哈洛尔德游记》、《唐璜》等，并在他的诗歌里塑造了一批“拜伦式英雄”。他不仅是一位伟大的诗人，还是一个为理想战斗一生的勇士，积极而勇敢地投身革命——参加了希腊民族解放运动，并成为领导人之一。拜伦女儿阿达·洛芙莱斯是计算机程序的创始人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 12px;padding-left: 12px;color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen为你</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">读诗</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;float: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;margin-top: -14px;background-color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;float: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;border-radius: 100%;float: right;margin-top: -14px;background-color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing:
